# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-30 02:33:30.171701

### Base Program

```py
def count_balls(low_limit: int, high_limit: int) -> int:
    box_counts = [0] * 46
    for i in range(low_limit, high_limit + 1):
        box_number = sum(map(int, str(i)))
        box_counts[box_number] += 1
    return max(box_counts)
```

### Input

```json
[32, 41]
```

## Test Case 1

### Modified Program

```py
def count_balls(low_limit: int, high_limit: int) -> int:
    box_counts = [0] * 46
    for i in range(low_limit, high_limit + 1):
        box_number = sum(map(int, str(i)))
        box_counts[box_number] += 1
    return max(box_counts)
```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py
def count_balls(var_0: int, var_1: int) -> int:
    box_counts = [0] * 46
    for i in range(var_0, var_1 + 1):
        box_number = sum(map(int, str(i)))
        box_counts[box_number] += 1
    return max(box_counts)
```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py
def count_balls(low_limit: int, high_limit: int) -> int:
    box_counts = 46 * [0]
    for i in range(low_limit, 1 + high_limit):
        box_number = sum(map(int, str(i)))
        box_counts[box_number] += 1
    return max(box_counts)
```

<details>
<summary>parser endpoint: passed ✅</summary>

Message: 
```
Success
```
